<div id="review_444585117" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/444585117" />
    <a title="Jane" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12037564-jane"><img alt="Jane" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408346116p2/12037564.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/444585117?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jane" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jane" href="/user/show/12037564-jane">Jane</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780615408989" href="/book/show/11382346-that-boy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12037564-jane?shelf=burn-in-hell">burn-in-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12037564-jane?shelf=god-save-the-queen">god-save-the-queen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12037564-jane?shelf=zero-stars">zero-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12037564-jane?shelf=not-even-sorry">not-even-sorry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12037564-jane?shelf=zzzzzzz">zzzzzzz</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer444585117" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8397230430513924883">This book is just absolute shit, don't waste your time. And I know I shouldn't be wasting mine by reviewing this piece of trash, but right now, I'm so FLABBERGASTED that such a <i>piece of literature</i> was even published and I need to let this whole thing out before I go out on the streets to practise some Jiu Jitsu.<br/><br/>So, <b>apparently</b>, this book is supposed to be about a love triangle between some "girl" who's "one of the boys" and two boys. We're told that she's pretty, she plays soccer soooo well, and </span>
  <span id="freeText8397230430513924883" style="display:none">This book is just absolute shit, don't waste your time. And I know I shouldn't be wasting mine by reviewing this piece of trash, but right now, I'm so FLABBERGASTED that such a <i>piece of literature</i> was even published and I need to let this whole thing out before I go out on the streets to practise some Jiu Jitsu.<br /><br />So, <b>apparently</b>, this book is supposed to be about a love triangle between some "girl" who's "one of the boys" and two boys. We're told that she's pretty, she plays soccer soooo well, and every single guy in the universe falls in love with her the moment she winks at them. What we're not told is that she’s whiny, she acts like a fifth-grader (except for the first few chapters where she acted like five), and spends most of her time on the prowl for cute guys. Not to mention Danny, one of the "love interests" (I'm scoffing at this) gets married off within the first half of the book. And for the rest of the book, she goes on and on and on and on about how naggy Philip (the other love interest) is and how she hates him and how every time she sees him, she feels like sticking her tongue down his throat and having sex with him. Like that's not enough, the author casually inserts five pages of "drama" into the book about her parents dying in a car accident. (Or was it getting stabbed by some gangsters? Wait, maybe they got eaten by some coyotes while on their twenty-year holiday in Africa.) Cue the whole crying on Philip's shoulder thing. BUT WAIT, that's not the end of this whole should-I-get-together-with-Philip-or-not drama, because after two pages, she goes on to date others guys in her college! Wow! I didn't even know she had graduated out of high school!<br /><br />Finally, when they get together, Philip proposes on their first date. He plans everything out exactly the way she told him was romantic. AND SHE SLAPS HIM. WTF? Is this woman bipolar or something?!<br /><br />As if the whole whack plot is not enough, the author decides to do some random bolding and underlining! Here I am reading, and suddenly, <u>
  <b>this huge bolded and underlined sentence pops up. It doesn’t even have any special meaning.</b>
</u> Plus the whole exclamation mark and question mark spam. Seriously, who talks like this????? No one!!!!!! For a twenty-two year old, it’s perfectly shameful to be talking like a dumb middle-schooler.<br /><br />This book was just horrible. The only thing that I am stumped by is how it managed to make me finish it. One thing for sure though, I am not going to read the sequel.<br /><br /><b>Edit</b>: WTF, did I read a pirated version of this book or something? Bloody hell, four point freaking zero nine stars for this piece of shit? Omg what.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/e3J45AjrNi03J4mFL+JRmelti6pguTDny41aqNoWA3Qc54uFauIdW6whDTV8/h/rZgcDwQFzjeOVMHWcgA25g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hgBSkTfZlBwLbT4Ia/EnChjd39jC2kA3uCZHOQM5qYyrngVcslGwsdEBJBqqvVYz0uB1+W9dasOpXLOF0lHHZw==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText5183373657364443992" style="display:none">Jillian is a <i>USA TODAY</i> bestselling author who writes fun romance novels with characters her readers fall in love with--from the boy next door in the That Boy trilogy, to the daughter of a famous actress in The Keatyn Chronicles®, to a kick-ass young assassin in the Spy Girl® series. Jillian's books have enthralled more than two million readers since she burst onto the indie scene in 2011.<br /><br />She lives in a small Florida beach town, is married to her college sweetheart, has two grown children, and two Labrador Retrievers named Cali and Camber. When she's not working, she likes to travel, paint, shop for shoes, watch football, and go to the beach.<br /><br />Check out Jillian’s website for added content: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jilliandodd.net">www.jilliandodd.net</a><br /><br /></span>
